<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports mouse, touch, and keyboard interactions on tabs</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports LTR and RTL keyboard navigation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Follows the tabs ARIA pattern, semantically linking tabs and their associated
tab panels</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Focus management for tab panels without any focusable children</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the tabs anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the tabs package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> tabs</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tabs&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The tabs package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

</span></div></pre><button type="button" class="px_2 py_1 gap_1 bd-w_1px pos_absolute right_5 top_3 d_flex ai_center fs_xs bg_bg.subtle bd-c_border.subtle cursor_pointer hover:bg_bg.muted"><svg stroke="currentColor" fill="none" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="w_1em h_1em va_middle" height="1em" width="1em" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M8 5H6a2 2 0 00-2 2v12a2 2 0 002 2h10a2 2 0 002-2v-1M8 5a2 2 0 002 2h2a2 2 0 002-2M8 5a2 2 0 012-2h2a2 2 0 012 2m0 0h2a2 2 0 012 2v3m2 4H10m0 0l3-3m-3 3l3 3"></path></svg><span>Copy</span></button></div></div></div>
<h3 id="setting-the-initially-selected-tab" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the initially selected tab<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-initially-selected-tab"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the initially selected tab, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> property to the
machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;tab-1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>Subsequently, you can use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.setValue</code> function to programmatically set
the selected tab.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;tab-2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>To clear selection (when <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">deselectable</code> is enabled), use:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">clearValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-tabs" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled tabs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-tabs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To control the selected tab programmatically, pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> properties to the machine function.</p>

<h3 id="changing-the-orientation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the orientation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-orientation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The default orientation of the tabs is horizontal. To change the orientation,
set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code> property in the machine&#x27;s context to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&quot;vertical&quot;</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">orientation</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;vertical&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="showing-an-indicator" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Showing an indicator<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#showing-an-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To show an active indicator when a tab is selected, you add the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">tabIndicatorProps</code> object provided by the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> function.</p>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token language-javascript"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getContentProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">value</span><span class="token operator">:</span> item<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>

<h3 id="disabling-a-tab" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabling a tab<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabling-a-tab"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To disable a tab, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code> property in the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getTriggerProps</code> to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<p>When a Tab is <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">disabled</code>, it is skipped during keyboard navigation and it is not
clickable.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>button</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getTriggerProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> <span class="token literal-property property">disabled</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;/</span>button</span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token comment">//...</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> — Callback invoked when the selected tab changes.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code> — Callback invoked when the focused tab changes.</li>
</ul>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allowing-deselection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing deselection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-deselection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">deselectable</code> to allow clicking the active tab to clear the current value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="custom-navigation-for-link-tabs" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Custom navigation for link tabs<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#custom-navigation-for-link-tabs"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">navigate</code> when your tab triggers are rendered as links.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    router<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">push</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">href</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>

<h3 id="manual-tab-activation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Manual tab activation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#manual-tab-activation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, a tab is selected when it receives focus from either keyboard or
pointer interaction. This is called &quot;automatic tab activation&quot;.</p>
<p>The other approach is &quot;manual tab activation&quot; which means the tab is selected
with the Enter key or by clicking on the tab.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">activationMode</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;manual&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="looping-keyboard-navigation" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Looping keyboard navigation<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#looping-keyboard-navigation"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code> to control whether arrow-key navigation wraps at the ends.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">loopFocus</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="rtl-support" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">RTL Support<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rtl-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tabs machine provides support right to left writing directions. In this
mode, the layout and keyboard interaction is flipped.</p>
<p>To enable RTL support, set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code> property in the machine&#x27;s context to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">rtl</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tabs<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">dir</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;rtl&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="programmatic-tab-control" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic tab control<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-tab-control"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the connected API for imperative navigation and focus.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">setValue</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;tab-2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">selectNext</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">selectPrev</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">focus</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="selected-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Selected state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#selected-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a tab is selected, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-selected</code> attribute is added to the trigger and
content elements.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;active&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for selected tab */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;content&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-state</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;active&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for selected tab */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a tab is disabled, a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute is added to the trigger
element.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for disabled tab */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="focused-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Focused state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#focused-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a tab is focused, you the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">:focus</code> or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">:focus-visible</code> pseudo-class to
style it.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token pseudo-class">:focus</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for focused tab */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>When any tab is focused, the list is given a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-focus</code> attribute.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-focus</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for when any tab is focused */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="orientation-styles" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Orientation styles<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#orientation-styles"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>All parts of the tabs component have the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-orientation</code> attribute. You can
use this to set the style for the horizontal or vertical tabs.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;trigger&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for horizontal/vertical tabs */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for horizontal/vertical root */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for horizontal/vertical tab-indicator */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;list&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-orientation</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;(horizontal|vertical)&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* Styles for horizontal/vertical list */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="the-tab-indicator" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">The tab indicator<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#the-tab-indicator"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tab indicator styles have CSS variables for the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">transitionDuration</code> and
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">transitionTimingFunction</code> defined in it.</p>
<p>The transition definition is applied when the selected tab changes to allow the
indicator move smoothly to the new selected tab.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;indicator&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--transition-duration</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> <span class="token number">0.2</span><span class="token unit">s</span><span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token variable">--transition-timing-function</span><span class="token punctuation">:</span> ease-in-out<span class="token punctuation">;</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tabs machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; trigger: (value: string) =&gt; string; list: string; content: (value: string) =&gt; string; indicator: string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the tabs. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">IntlTranslations</code><span class="d_block">Specifies the localized strings that identifies the accessibility elements and their states</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loopFocus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the keyboard navigation will loop from last tab to first, and vice versa.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The controlled selected tab value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial selected tab value when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the selected tab value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">orientation</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;horizontal&quot; | &quot;vertical&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The orientation of the tabs. Can be `horizontal` or `vertical`
- `horizontal`: only left and right arrow key navigation will work.
- `vertical`: only up and down arrow key navigation will work.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">activationMode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;manual&quot; | &quot;automatic&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The activation mode of the tabs. Can be `manual` or `automatic`
- `manual`: Tabs are activated when clicked or press `enter` key.
- `automatic`: Tabs are activated when receiving focus</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ValueChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback to be called when the selected/active tab changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: FocusChangeDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Callback to be called when the focused tab changes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">composite</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tab is composite</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">deselectable</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether the active tab can be deselected when clicking on it.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">navigate</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: NavigateDetails) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to navigate to the selected tab when clicking on it.
Useful if tab triggers are anchor elements.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;ltr&quot; | &quot;rtl&quot;</code><span class="d_block">The document&#x27;s text/writing direction.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The unique identifier of the machine.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getRootNode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; ShadowRoot | Node | Document</code><span class="d_block">A root node to correctly resolve document in custom environments. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tabs <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The current value of the tabs.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focusedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The value of the tab that is currently focused.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the value of the tabs.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Clears the value of the tabs.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setIndicatorRect</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the indicator rect to the tab with the given value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">syncTabIndex</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Synchronizes the tab index of the content element.
Useful when rendering tabs within a select or combobox</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focus</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Set focus on the selected tab trigger</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectNext</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(fromValue?: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Selects the next tab</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectPrev</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(fromValue?: string) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Selects the previous tab</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getTriggerState</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(props: TriggerProps) =&gt; TriggerState</code><span class="d_block">Returns the state of the trigger with the given props</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="data-attributes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Data Attributes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#data-attributes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Root</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column panels.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/tabs\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"Tabs\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Supports mouse, touch, and keyboard interactions on tabs\n- Supports LTR and RTL keyboard navigation\n- Follows the tabs ARIA pattern, semantically linking tabs and their associated\n  tab panels\n- Focus management for tab panels without any focusable children\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the tabs package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tabs/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the tabs anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"tabs\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the tabs package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as tabs from \"@zag-js/tabs\"\n```\n\nThe tabs package exports two key functions:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tabs/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting the initially selected tab\n\nTo set the initially selected tab, pass the `defaultValue` property to the\nmachine's context.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  defaultValue: \"tab-1\",\n})\n```\n\nSubsequently, you can use the `api.setValue` function to programmatically set\nthe selected tab.\n\n```jsx\napi.setValue(\"tab-2\")\n```\n\nTo clear selection (when `deselectable` is enabled), use:\n\n```jsx\napi.clearValue()\n```\n\n### Controlled tabs\n\nTo control the selected tab programmatically, pass the `value` and\n`onValueChange` properties to the machine function.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tabs/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Changing the orientation\n\nThe default orientation of the tabs is horizontal. To change the orientation,\nset the `orientation` property in the machine's context to `\"vertical\"`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  orientation: \"vertical\",\n})\n```\n\n### Showing an indicator\n\nTo show an active indicator when a tab is selected, you add the\n`tabIndicatorProps` object provided by the `connect` function.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"tabs/with-indicator.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Disabling a tab\n\nTo disable a tab, set the `disabled` property in the `getTriggerProps` to\n`true`.\n\nWhen a Tab is `disabled`, it is skipped during keyboard navigation and it is not\nclickable.\n\n```jsx\n//...\n\u003cbutton {...api.getTriggerProps({ disabled: true })}\u003e\u003c/button\u003e\n//...\n```\n\n### Listening for events\n\n- `onValueChange` — Callback invoked when the selected tab changes.\n- `onFocusChange` — Callback invoked when the focused tab changes.\n\n```jsx {2-7}\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focusedValue: string }\n    console.log(\"focused tab:\", details.focusedValue)\n  },\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string }\n    console.log(\"selected tab:\", details.value)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Allowing deselection\n\nSet `deselectable` to allow clicking the active tab to clear the current value.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  deselectable: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Custom navigation for link tabs\n\nUse `navigate` when your tab triggers are rendered as links.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  navigate(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string, node: HTMLAnchorElement, href: string }\n    router.push(details.href)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Manual tab activation\n\nBy default, a tab is selected when it receives focus from either keyboard or\npointer interaction. This is called \"automatic tab activation\".\n\nThe other approach is \"manual tab activation\" which means the tab is selected\nwith the Enter key or by clicking on the tab.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  activationMode: \"manual\",\n})\n```\n\n### Looping keyboard navigation\n\nSet `loopFocus` to control whether arrow-key navigation wraps at the ends.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  loopFocus: false,\n})\n```\n\n### RTL Support\n\nThe tabs machine provides support right to left writing directions. In this\nmode, the layout and keyboard interaction is flipped.\n\nTo enable RTL support, set the `dir` property in the machine's context to `rtl`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(tabs.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n```\n\n### Programmatic tab control\n\nUse the connected API for imperative navigation and focus.\n\n```jsx\napi.setValue(\"tab-2\")\napi.selectNext()\napi.selectPrev()\napi.focus()\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\n### Selected state\n\nWhen a tab is selected, a `data-selected` attribute is added to the trigger and\ncontent elements.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-state=\"active\"] {\n  /* Styles for selected tab */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"content\"][data-state=\"active\"] {\n  /* Styles for selected tab */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen a tab is disabled, a `data-disabled` attribute is added to the trigger\nelement.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* Styles for disabled tab */\n}\n```\n\n### Focused state\n\nWhen a tab is focused, you the `:focus` or `:focus-visible` pseudo-class to\nstyle it.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"]:focus {\n  /* Styles for focused tab */\n}\n```\n\nWhen any tab is focused, the list is given a `data-focus` attribute.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"list\"][data-focus] {\n  /* Styles for when any tab is focused */\n}\n```\n\n### Orientation styles\n\nAll parts of the tabs component have the `data-orientation` attribute. You can\nuse this to set the style for the horizontal or vertical tabs.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"trigger\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* Styles for horizontal/vertical tabs */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* Styles for horizontal/vertical root */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"indicator\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* Styles for horizontal/vertical tab-indicator */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"list\"][data-orientation=\"(horizontal|vertical)\"] {\n  /* Styles for horizontal/vertical list */\n}\n```\n\n### The tab indicator\n\nThe tab indicator styles have CSS variables for the `transitionDuration` and\n`transitionTimingFunction` defined in it.\n\nThe transition definition is applied when the selected tab changes to allow the\nindicator move smoothly to the new selected tab.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"indicator\"] {\n  --transition-duration: 0.2s;\n  --transition-timing-function: ease-in-out;\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe tabs machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"tabs\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe tabs `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"tabs\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"tabs\" /\u003e\n\n### CSS Variables\n\n\u003cCssVarTable name=\"tabs\" /\u003e\n\n## Accessibility\n\n### Keyboard Interactions\n\n\u003cKeyboardTable name=\"tabs\" /\u003e"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"5:[\"$\",\"$Le\",null,{\"doc\":{\"title\":\"Tabs\",\"description\":\"Using the tabs machine in your
